This function:\\n\\n1. **Extracts gRPC status**: Uses `grpcstatus.FromError(err)` to extract the gRPC status from an error\\n2. **Maps to HTTP**: Switches on `s.Code()` to map gRPC codes to HTTP status codes:\\n   - `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound` (404)\\n   - `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests` (429) with Retry-After header\\n   - Default → `http.StatusInternalServerError` (500)\\n3. **Writes response**: Calls `w.WriteHeader(status)` and `w.Write()` to send the HTTP response\\n\\nGRPC errors are created directly in service implementations. Extracts gRPC status from downstream service errors: `status.FromError(err)`\\n   - Switches on error code to map to backend response status:\\n     - `codes.InvalidArgument` → `backend.StatusBadRequest`\\n     - `codes.PermissionDenied` → `backend.StatusForbidden`\\n     - `codes.NotFound` → `backend.StatusNotFound`\\n     - `codes.Unavailable` → `http.StatusServiceUnavailable`\\n     - `codes.Unauthenticated` → `backend.StatusUnauthorized`\\n\\n4. **Resource Authorization Errors** (`pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go`, lines 596-598, 1022-1024):\\n   - `ErrGRPCMemberNotFound = status.Error(codes.NotFound, ...)`  (line 46)\\n   - `ErrGRPCRequestTooManyRequests = status.Error(codes.ResourceExhausted, ...)`  (line 57)\\n   - `ErrGRPCPermissionDenied = status.Error(codes.PermissionDenied, ...)`  (line 69)\\n   - Enables reconstructing the same gRPC error from its string representation\\n\\n3. **Server-side Error Translation** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go`, lines 35-108):\\n   - `toGRPCErrorMap` (lines 35-96) maps internal server errors to gRPC errors:\\n     - `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `rpctypes.ErrGRPCMemberNotFound`\\n     - `mvcc.ErrCompacted` → `rpctypes.ErrGRPCCompacted`\\n     - `errors.ErrNoLeader` → `rpctypes.ErrGRPCNoLeader`\\n   - `togRPCError()` function (lines 98-108) performs the actual translation:\\n     - Allows context cancellation/deadline errors to pass through\\n     - Uses the map to convert, or defaults to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)`\\n\\n4. **RPC Handler Integration** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/auth.go`, `key.go`, `member.go`, `lease.go`, `maintenance.go`):\\n   - All RPC handlers call `togRPCError()` when returning errors\\n   - Example from auth.go (line 37-38): `if err != nil { return nil, togRPCError(err) }`\\n   - Example from member.go (line 104-106): `if err != nil { return nil, togRPCError(err) }`\\n\\n5. **HTTP Bridge** (`server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go`, lines 152-159):\\n   - Translates gRPC errors to HTTP responses for HTTP endpoints\\n   - Maps specific error types to HTTP status codes:\\n     - `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n     - `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n**Kubernetes**: Uses inline error creation at service boundaries and translation at the streaming handler layer.\\n\\n**Grafana**: Uses both direct gRPC error creation in interceptors and unified conversion functions for downstream error translation.\\n\\n**etcd**: Uses a centralized, declarative approach with pre-defined error constants and a single conversion function (`togRPCError`) that all RPC handlers invoke consistently.\\n\\nThe etcd approach is the most maintainable because it centralizes error definitions and conversions, while Kubernetes and Grafana distribute error creation throughout their codebases and translate at multiple points (interceptors, handlers, and gateway layers).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4182,"cache_read_input_tokens":87383,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4182},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"70cf3bbc-dd87-4cd8-8209-92499f84e774","uuid":"a01ccb83-c811-4999-938a-a98950156ce5"}

Translates gRPC errors to HTTP responses for HTTP endpoints\\n   - Maps specific error types to HTTP status codes:\\n     - `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n     - `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n**Kubernetes**: Uses inline error creation at service boundaries and translation at the streaming handler layer.\\n\\n**Grafana**: Uses both direct gRPC error creation in interceptors and unified conversion functions for downstream error translation.\\n\\n**etcd**: Uses a centralized, declarative approach with pre-defined error constants and a single conversion function (`togRPCError`) that all RPC handlers invoke consistently.\\n\\nThe etcd approach is the most maintainable because it centralizes error definitions and conversions, while Kubernetes and Grafana distribute error creation throughout their codebases and translate at multiple points (interceptors, handlers, and gateway layers).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
